Accessibility digest

Synopsis
PageWellTower partner Sagora Senior Living

Requesterpool@jpdev.pro

Score1668
Tested byTestaro, procedure ts24
Scored byTestilo, procedure tsp24
Digested byTestilo, procedure tdp24

Introduction

This is a digest of results from a battery of accessibility Tests.

The battery includes 1353 automated accessibility tests drawn from ten different packages: Alfa, Axe, Continuum, Equal Access, HTML CodeSniffer, Nu Html Checker, QualWeb, Tenon, Testaro, and WAVE.

These tests were run on the web page named above and gave the page a score of 1668, where 0 would be perfect.

Issue summary

Special issues

log: Score 267. This is based on the amount of browser error logging and miscellaneous logging during the tests.

preventions: Score 100. This is based on tests that the page did not allow to be run. That impedes accessibility progress and risks interfering with tools that users with disabilities need.

solos: Score 4. This is based on issues reported by unclassified tests. Details are in the report.

Classified issues

Issue linkNoText

WCAG: 2.4.4

Score: 244

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package alfa, test r11, score 20 (Link has no accessible name)
  • Package axe, test link-name, score 30 (Link has no discernible text)
  • Package continuum, test 237, score 20 (a element has no mechanism that allows an accessible name value to be calculated)
  • Package htmlcs, test e:AAA.4_1_2.H91.A.EmptyNoId, score 4 (Link has no name or id attribute or value)
  • Package htmlcs, test e:AAA.4_1_2.H91.A.NoContent, score 20 (Link has an href attribute but no text)
  • Package ibm, test WCAG20_A_HasText, score 20 (Hyperlink has no text description)
  • Package wave, test e:alt_link_missing, score 120 (Linked image has no text alternative)
  • Package wave, test e:link_empty, score 20 (Link contains no text)
  • Package tenon, test 57, score 140 (Link has no text inside it)

Issue linkForcesNewWindow

WCAG: 3.2.5

Score: 116

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package tenon, test 218, score 114 (Link opens in a new window without user control)

Issue focusableHidden

WCAG: 4.1.2

Score: 102

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package tenon, test 194, score 100 (Visible element is focusable but has a presentation role or aria-hidden=true attribute)

Score: 86

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package ibm, test Rpt_Aria_WidgetLabels_Implicit, score 84 (Interactive component has no programmatically associated name)

Applying `role=\"presentation\"` removes the semantics of an element, while `aria-hidden=\"true\"` hides an element from assistive technology only. Neither completely hides an element. Their application to a focusable element creates confusion in users of assistive technology.
